What I especially like about this book is the lack of entirely happy ending and it's use of the loved literary technique, the cl</span>
  <span id="freeText665826901271751952" style="display:none">I saw this book was free on kindle and HAD to get it. Thankfully, I was not disappointed. With an intriguing plot line, interesting characters, and pieces from at least 10 different genres this book has something for everyone! The characters can easily be identified with (not the mindreading aspect) and showcase a wide array of qualities typical of the character's age. What I especially like about this book is the lack of entirely happy ending and it's use of the loved literary technique, the cliffhanger. A fast paced read recommended to 13-18 year olds. 4 out of 5 stars.<br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722221553" />
    <a title="Susan ...so many books and so little time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10067939-susan-so-many-books-and-so-little-time"><img alt="Susan ...so many books and so little time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606234737p2/10067939.jpg" /></a>

On to the next book...</span>

<div id="review_268556138" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/268556138" />
    <a title="Heather *Undercover Goth Queen*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen"><img alt="Heather *Undercover Goth Queen*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565231860p2/1256869.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/268556138?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather *Undercover Goth Queen*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather *Undercover Goth Queen*" href="/user/show/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen">Heather *Undercover Goth Queen*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9884118-the-mind-readers">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=2012">2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=other-supernatural">other-supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1256869-heather-undercover-goth-queen?shelf=free">free</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268556138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14547931966710711119">In the beginning, I was actually skeptical of this book and really thought I wouldn't like it. While I do think it could have used more development all around—the setting, the characters, motivations, etc.—I found myself getting very interested in the latter half of the book. I really liked how the author brought the story around at the end. I'm looking forward to the next book in the series.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SO04A/8zLLdc1PAU+BioXH3wbYMVQGvOoHhPg8J92mAVj+JPexdhKV3rDEPFWYc/l4eNPiohjHf8Q4kdplj7xw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5J1OT3drzgYY+0Bm2tDrZpaCka5IZWFzCBwT7lnyGay5/5QD80+DmBnEvDHnkcQFfPVxE3cEhspUJ9VwPdc4Cw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2919562.Lori_Brighton">About Lori Brighton</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8646277869526326554">As a child, thoughts of far-off places and adventure consistently kept Lori up late at night. After graduating high school, she came to the conclusion that there was no better way to seek adventure and nourish her love of history than to become an archaeologist. She went on to receive a degree in anthropology, but digging in the dirt during humid Midwestern summers wasn’t exactly as fun as she tho</span>
  <span id="freeText8646277869526326554" style="display:none">As a child, thoughts of far-off places and adventure consistently kept Lori up late at night. After graduating high school, she came to the conclusion that there was no better way to seek adventure and nourish her love of history than to become an archaeologist. She went on to receive a degree in anthropology, but digging in the dirt during humid Midwestern summers wasn’t exactly as fun as she thought it would be.<br /><br />Instead, she went to work in an air conditioned museum where she spent her days surrounded by creepy Victorian animal mounts. Still, she wasn’t satisfied. <br /><br />Deciding the people in her imagination were slightly more exciting than the dead things in a museum basement, she set out to write her first romance novel. That book was soundly rejected. As was the next. Years went by and she began to wonder if she’d ever see her dream fulfilled. Until one day she came up with an idea for a book that brought together her love of history and adventure: a book now titled Wild Heart. Since Wild Heart's release, Lori has written Historical Romance, Contemporary Paranormal Romance and Young Adult. <br /><br />Lori currently resides in the Southern U.S., where she juggles her time between a husband, a son, a golden retriever, a cat and the many, many people in her imagination. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8646277869526326554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Perhaps someday she can forget the pain she has endured…if only the past would stop haunting her. \n\nBefore she can truly move on and accept the relative normalcy of her new life, there are a few things she has to uncover. But Maddox is the least of her worries when someone starts stalking Nora’s every move…a woman who looks eerily like her dead mother. For Nora, time is running out.
